 indian railway cataring and tourism corporation (iarsitisi) 21 november se rail aadhaarit saptahik yatra package shuru karegaa, jisase samay bachaane kii chahat rakhane vaale yatri teen shatabdi express trainon se teen aitihaasik evam jeevant shahar - dilli, agra or jaipur -svarnim tribhuj- kii yatra kar sakenge
 The tickets for the three Shatabdi Express trains have been added as part of the two-day rail travel package initiative from Delhi to Agra and Jaipur, to provide a comfortable and hassle-free itinerary to the passengers
 iarsitisi ke pramukh or prabandh nideshak eke manocha ne kaha, yah un abhinav yatra packejon main se ek he, jo kam samay ke safar kii yojana banane vaale yatriyon ke puri tarah anukool he
 With the package, travelers can experience the grandeur of some of the most famous monuments in the country
 shatabdi trainen bhartiya rail network kii sabase tej raftaar vaali trainon main se ek hai or in vaataanukoolit trainon main bhojan bhi uplabdh karaayaa jaataa he
 The package is for every Saturday and Sunday and will start on 21 November
 ek raat-do din ke 'golden triengal package' ke tahat nai dilli stesan par tadake mehmaan dilli-habibganj shatabdi main savaar honge or agra main train chodenge
 As part of the package, passengers will be shown the Taj Mahal of Agra, the tomb of Itmad ud Daulah, Agra Fort and will be served lunch at a five-star hotel in the city
 iske baad ve agra-jaipur shatabdi main savaar hokar subah jaipur pahunchenge
 The comments unhen jaipur main bhi prasiddh sthalon kii saiyr karaayi jaaegi
 And from there, he will return to Delhi by boarding the jaipur-new Delhi Shatabdi Express
 sabhi sthalon ke liye unhen vaataanukoolit gadiyon main le jaaya jayega
 The per person cost of the package, with two passengers, is Rs 9,444 and does not include the entrance fee for the monuments
 package kii booking iarsitisi ke paryaton portal par kii ja sakati he
 For more information, one can call 1800110139, which is a toll free number
 dilli se agra or jaipur kii do din kii rail yatra package pahal ke tahat teen shatabdi express trainon ke tikat aapas main jod die gaye hai, taaki yatriyon ko ek aaraamdeh evam pareshaani mukt yatra kaarykram uplabdh karaayaa ja sake
 IRCTC chief and managing director AK Manocha said, "it is one of those innovative travel packages that is perfectly suited for travelers planning short-haul travel
" package se yatri desh ke kuch sabase prasiddh smarakon kii bhavyata kaa anubhav kar sakate hai
 Shatabdi trains are one of the fastest trains on the Indian rail network and food is also provided in these air-conditioned trains
 package har shanivaar or ravivaar ke liye he or 21 november se shuru hoga
 Guests will board the delhi-habibganj Shatabdi and leave the train at Agra in the early hours of a two-day 'golden Triangle Package' at New Delhi station
 package ke tahat yatriyon ko agra kaa tajmahal, itmaad ud daula kaa makbara, agra kila dikhaaya jayega or shahar ke ek paanch sitara hotel main dopaher kaa bhojan karaayaa jayega

 tippaniyan They will also be visited famous places in Jaipur

 The initiative was taken at the 1992 United Nations Conference on Environment and Development (UN CED) in Rio de Janeiro, Brazil
 jal sankat sambandhi kuch tathy:- duniya kii 17 fisadi aabaadi bharat main he
 But only 4 percent of the world's clean water is in the country

 According to the government report, the demand for water in India is increasing at the rate of 830 billion cubic meters (BCM) every year
 lekin pani kii aapurti 1,123 bisiem par hi sthir he
 In a few years, this supply will fall to 1000 BCM
